### [83] [Generalized Schwarzian Dynamics from a Bulk-First BF Perspective](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15270)
*H. T. Özer,Aytül Filiz*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文从BF引力的体视角出发，研究广义Schwarzian动力学的涌现，通过Drinfeld-Sokolov约化，在sl(2,R)和sl(3,R)情形下分别恢复标准Schwarzian作用量及由Wilczynski不变量描述的高秩推广，并将其与Casimir荷、单值性数据和广义Schwarzian热力学联系起来。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解广义Schwarzian动力学如何从体理论（特别是BF引力）自然涌现，而非作为独立边界理论人为引入。

Method: 基于二维BF引力，分析其边界相空间及其Drinfeld-Sokolov约化；对sl(2,R)和sl(3,R)情形分别推导约化后的边界动力学，并关联到Wilczynski不变量、Casimir荷、单值性及热力学结构。

Result: 在sl(2,R)中重现标准Schwarzian作用量；在sl(3,R)中得到由第二、第三Wilczynski不变量主导的动力学；建立项目几何不变量与Casimir荷、单值谱及半经典热力学之间的系统联系。

Conclusion: 广义Schwarzian动力学可直接从平直BF联络及其伴随形式中导出；该框架统一了Schwarzian类动力学的体起源，揭示了BF引力、渐近对称性约化、射影几何与边界热力学间的深刻联系。

Abstract: We investigate the emergence of generalized Schwarzian dynamics from a bulk-first BF perspective. Starting from two-dimensional BF gravity, we analyze the associated boundary phase space and its Drinfeld-Sokolov reductions. For the sl(2,R) theory, we recover the ordinary Schwarzian action as the reduced boundary dynamics arising from a particular sector of the BF asymptotic phase space. We then extend this construction to sl(3,R), where the reduced dynamics is governed by the second and third Wilczynski invariants, providing a natural higher-rank generalization of the Schwarzian derivative. In this framework, generalized Schwarzian dynamics emerges directly from flat BF connections and their companion forms rather than being introduced as an independent boundary theory. We further relate the resulting projective invariants to Casimir charges, monodromy data, and generalized Schwarzian thermodynamics, including monodromy spectra and semiclassical thermodynamics. In particular, constant projective invariants determine the corresponding Casimir sectors and monodromy data, which in turn organize the thermodynamic structure of the theory. Our results provide a unified bulk-first description of Schwarzian and generalized Schwarzian dynamics and reveal a direct link between BF gravity, asymptotic symmetry reductions, projective geometry, and boundary thermodynamics.

Abstract: We study the evaporation and Page curve of charged near-AdS$_2$ black holes coupled to a non-gravitating bath at fixed temperature and chemical potential. The low-energy dynamics is governed by the Schwarzian reparametrization mode together with a $U(1)$ phase mode. We average the boundary energy and the outgoing flux over these two soft modes and obtain corrected balance equations for the temperature and chemical potential. We then use the corrected background to calculate the no-island and island entropies and the Page time shifts. We find that the two soft sectors affect the Page transition in our low-temperature semiclassical regime. The $U(1)$ phase mode correction delays the Page transition, while the Schwarzian correction tends to move it earlier. The total Page time shift is therefore determined by the competition between the Schwarzian and $U(1)$ sectors.

We also study the possibility of black hole formation and gravitational wave background in this scenario. We find that in the case when the symmetry breaking field does not backreact on inflation, black hole production is not feasible. However, under specific conditions, gravitational waves fitting the NANOGrav band can be obtained.

### [86] [Flat Gauging of Continuous (Non-invertible) Symmetries and Non-compact BF SymTFT for Compact Boson](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15732)

Motivation: 理解连续对称性平直规范的物理效应，特别是其对紧致玻色子理论结构、退紧致化、对偶性及模空间的影响，并拓展至非可逆对称性和SymTFT框架。

Method: 通过构造环面配分函数分析平直U(1)_M × U(1)_W规范；利用混合反常和对偶性论证退紧致化机制；在自对偶半径下研究SO(3)平直规范及其连续orbifold；分析非可逆规范中的零测度不动点问题；将SymTFT建模为非紧致BF理论并关联Narain模空间与T-对偶。

Result: 平直规范单个U(1)导致退紧致化；混合反常使剩余U(1)与对偶ℤ背景合成ℝ对称性背景；SO(3)平直规范生成超出c=1模空间的连续orbifold；连续非可逆规范需特殊处理零测度不动点；SymTFT被实现为非紧致BF理论，统一描述Narain模空间与O(D,D;ℤ)对称性。

Conclusion: 平直规范是探索连续对称性、反常、对偶与模空间结构的有力工具；其不仅引发退紧致化与新orbifold分支，还自然导向SymTFT的BF描述，为理解弦论与凝聚态中高阶对称性提供统一框架。

Abstract: We study flat gauging of continuous symmetries by summing over flat gauge-field configurations. We focus on the two-dimensional compact boson and construct the torus partition function with general flat $U(1)_M\times U(1)_W$ backgrounds. We show that flat gauging either $U(1)_M$ or $U(1)_W$ decompactifies the theory to the non-compact free boson, and that the dual $\mathbb{Z}$ background combines with the remaining $U(1)$ background into a non-compact $\mathbb{R}$ symmetry background due to the mixed anomaly. We also revisit the self-dual radius, where flat gauging the diagonal $SO(3)\subset (SU(2)_L\times SU(2)_R)/\mathbb{Z}_2$, first pointed out by Gaberdiel and Suchanek, gives the continuous orbifold which lies outside the usual $c=1$ moduli space. On the orbifold branch, we study finite and continuous non-invertible flat gaugings and explain why the continuous case requires a prescription for zero-measure fixed loci on the moduli space. Finally, we formulate the SymTFT of torus sigma models as a non-compact BF theory, whose topological boundary states encode the Narain moduli space and the $O(D,D;\mathbb{Z})$ T-duality action.

### [87] [Entanglement islands of 2D charged scalar-hairy black holes on the brane](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15792)
*Qingsong Li,Yuxuan Liu,Wenjie Zhu*

Main category: hep-th

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解双全息框架下带物质场（Maxwell场和标量场）的低维膜黑洞在热环境中的量子纠缠演化行为，特别是Page曲线如何受不同物质源影响。

Method: 采用岛公式（island formula）计算纠缠熵，分析电荷与标量源对膜上有效张力及自由度的影响，并研究其对Page时间和纠缠动力学的作用。

Result: 电荷增强全局有效张力、提高饱和熵；标量源削弱红外区域局部有效张力、抑制纠缠；纠缠演化分早时二次增长与晚时线性增长两个阶段；Page时间受温度（加速）与自由度（延迟）共同调控。

Conclusion: 即使存在物质场的非平凡回响，2D膜MS黑洞的纠缠动力学仍具有鲁棒性；不同物质源对Page曲线的调控机制可归结为对膜上自由度的有效调控，揭示了低维引力系统中信息恢复过程的关键物理参数。

Abstract: We investigate the entanglement dynamics and Page curve of a 2D brane Maxwell-Scalar (MS) black hole coupled to thermal baths in double holography. Computing the entanglement entropy via the island formula, we find that injecting electric charge and scalar source into the system produce opposite effects: the former increases the degrees of freedom (DOF) on the brane by enhancing the effective global tension, thereby raising the saturation entropy of the system; conversely, the latter reduces the DOF on the brane by lowering the effective local tension near the IR geometry, ultimately suppressing the entanglement. Despite the non-trivial backreaction from the matter fields, the pre-saturation entanglement dynamics remain robust. We identify an early-time quadratic growth corresponding to the pre-local-thermalization phase, which smoothly transitions into a late-time linear growth. Furthermore, the scale of the Page time is governed by a competition between thermal excitations and the brane DOF. Higher temperatures accelerate the onset of the Page time by exciting more Hawking modes, while abundant DOF delay it by increasing the saturated entropy.

*Meseret Asrat*

Main category: hep-th

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过构造Lax联络和经典r-矩阵，验证模型满足经典Yang-Baxter方程；分析其代数结构，确认其基于Z-分次非李Malcev代数；关联Poisson-Boltzmann方程导出相关可积模型族。

Result: 确立了一个新的二维经典可积模型，明确其Lax表示与r-矩阵结构；揭示其代数背景为共享Cartan子代数的sl(2,R)直和构成的Malcev代数；给出一族与Poisson-Boltzmann方程相关的经典可积模型。

Abstract: In this paper we present an integrable model in two dimensions. It is a deformation of the sine(sinh)-Gordon model. We give its Lax connection. We also obtain its (classical) $r$-matrix. It satisfies the classical Yang-Baxter equation. Thus, the model is a classical integrable field theory in two dimensions. The underlying algebra is a ${\cal Z}$-graded non-Lie Malcev algebra. It is a direct sum of $sl(2, {\rm I\!R})$ Lie algebras with a shared common Cartan. A Malcev algebra is the tangent space at the identity of an analytic Moufang loop as a Lie algebra is the tangent space at the identity of a Lie group. We expect the model to be integrable at the quantum level. We also give a family of classically integrable models which are related to the Poisson-Boltzmann equation in two dimensions.

Abstract: Four-dimensional gauge and gravitational theories exhibit long-range interactions that require asymptotic particles to be dressed by clouds of soft photons and gravitons. We show that this loss of Fock-space factorisation is not fundamental, but reflects an inappropriate choice of infrared variables. The real soft divergence is reproduced by the Goldstone modes of asymptotic symmetries, while the Coulomb phase is reproduced by new zero modes of the radiative fields that we introduce here. In these variables, infrared-finite dressed multi-particle states admit the usual Fock-space factorisation into single-particle dressed states.

Result: 成功构造出首个显式的O(4)-破缺真空衰变解：两个正负号相反、缠绕正交环的气泡管；该解具有有效实时间初值，并拥有奇数个不稳定模。

Conclusion: O(4)-对称性并非真空衰变的必然要求；存在具有更丰富几何结构和拓扑性质的非径向衰变通道，可能影响早期宇宙相变动力学。

Abstract: False vacuum decay in field theory is thought to be dominated by Coleman's O(4)-symmetric bounce, the minimum action nontrivial solution of the imaginary time equations of motion. Beyond the bounce, non-constructive existence proofs of O(4)-breaking solutions are available in the mathematics literature, but the solutions themselves, and their physics, have remained unknown. Considering the simple, bounded-below, scalar field potential $V(φ)=\frac{m^2}{2}φ^2-\fracλ{4}φ^4+\frac{g}{6}φ^6$, we construct a nonradial solution explicitly: two bubble-tubes of opposite sign wrapping orthogonal rings, invariant under ${\rm O}(2)\times{\rm O}(2)$ rotations combined with a parity that exchanges the rings. The solution admits valid Cauchy data for real time evolution from a $t=0$ slice, and supports an odd number of unstable deformation modes.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 由于在引力存在下，自相互作用标量场理论无法在没有非最小耦合的情况下重整化，因此引入曲率-标量非最小耦合以解决该问题。

Method: 使用微扰量子引力计算，建模大质量物体为非相对论性标量场，并在eikonal近似下计算2-2散射过程，得到弯曲角至O(ξG²)精度。

Result: 发现树图级（O(ξG)）无弯曲效应，O(ξG²)为领头阶；弯曲角随碰撞参数b呈b⁻⁷行为；非最小耦合顶点与标准最小耦合顶点在动量依赖结构上有本质区别。

Conclusion: 非最小耦合显著改变了引力弯曲行为，其弯曲角标度律和顶点结构均不同于标准最小耦合情形，凸显了非最小耦合在量子引力效应中的关键作用。

Abstract: We investigate the bending of massless fields by a massive object in the presence of a curvature-scalar $\sqrt{-g}ξR φ^2$ non-minimal coupling up to one loop, using the perturbative quantum gravity computations. It is well known that without such coupling a self interacting scalar field theory cannot be renormalised in the presence of gravity. The massive object is modelled by a massive scalar $φ$, and it is assumed to be non-relativistic, e.g., a star. We compute the 2-2 scattering of massless scalar and photons off this object via graviton exchanges. Assuming both $ξ$ and the bending angle to be small, we use the eikonal approximation to compute the angle up to ${\cal O}(ξG^2)$. At tree level $({\cal O}(ξG))$ we find no bending, and hence the ${\cal O}(ξG^2)$ result happens to be leading in this case. The non-minimal vertices are qualitatively different from that of the standard minimal ones, e.g. $ \sqrt{G} h_{μν} T^{μν}$, as the former contains explicit momenta of the gravitons instead of the scalar, complementing the second. The bending angle is found to behave like $\sim b^{-7}$, where $b$ is the impact parameter. We have emphasised the qualitative differences of our results from that of the well studied minimal case.

*Yannick Mvondo-She*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于复化Virasoro演化的几何解释，用于理解拓扑质量引力中对数引力子所体现的Jordan结构，并将其与边界对数共形场论（LCFT）中的不可分解结构相联系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解AdS₃/LCFT₂对应中对数引力子的几何本质及其与边界LCFT中对数伙伴的关联。

Method: 基于Grumiller-Johansson对数引力子解，分析其对数系数在AdS₃边界附近的渐近形式；引入复参数s = ρ + iτ，将Virasoro生成元L₀作用于rank-two Jordan块的指数演化e^{sL₀}与该几何结构关联；通过解析延拓揭示对数单值性。

Result: 发现径向演化、时间演化、Jordan混合与对数单值性均为同一复化Virasoro流的不同表现；为LCFT中不可分解结构提供了几何诠释；深化了对数引力子在AdS₃/LCFT₂框架下的物理意义。

Conclusion: 复化Virasoro演化统一刻画了对数引力子的Jordan结构，为AdS₃/LCFT₂对应提供了新的几何视角，并强化了LCFT不可分解性与引力理论之间的深层联系。

Abstract: At the chiral point of topologically massive gravity, the massive graviton becomes degenerate with the left-moving graviton, leading to the appearance of a logarithmic mode and a corresponding rank-two Jordan structure. This logarithmic graviton plays a central role in the conjectured AdS$_3$/LCFT$_2$ correspondence, where it has been widely interpreted as the bulk counterpart of a logarithmic partner in the putative boundary logarithmic conformal field theory. In this work, we develop a geometric interpretation of this Jordan structure based on complexified Virasoro evolution. Starting from the logarithmic graviton of Grumiller and Johansson, we show that its logarithmic coefficient \[ y(τ,ρ) =
-iτ-\ln\coshρ\] admits, near the AdS$_3$ boundary, the asymptotic form \[ y(τ,ρ) =
-s+\ln2+\mathcal O(e^{-2ρ}), \qquad s=ρ+iτ. \] The same complex parameter naturally appears in the exponentiation of the Virasoro generator $L_0$ acting on a rank-two Jordan cell, \[ L_0=h\mathbf1+N, \qquad N^2=0, \] for which \[ e^{sL_0} =
e^{sh}(1+sN). \] We show that the resulting Jordan evolution reproduces the characteristic logarithmic mixing of the logarithmic sector, while analytic continuation $s\rightarrow s+2πi$ generates the corresponding logarithmic monodromy. From this perspective, radial evolution, temporal evolution, Jordan mixing, and logarithmic monodromy may be viewed as different manifestations of a single complexified Virasoro flow. The analysis suggests a geometric interpretation of the indecomposable structures characteristic of logarithmic conformal field theory and offers a new perspective on the logarithmic graviton within the conjectural AdS$_3$/LCFT$_2$ framework.

### [95] [Holographic study of heavy quark potential, free energy, and running coupling in backgrounds with broken translational symmetry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.16640)

Method: 基于具有平移对称性破缺（TSB）的五维渐近AdS时空，采用Einstein-Maxwell-axion几何框架，数值模拟有限温与零温下的静态夸克势、热自由能和跑动耦合常数。

Result: 化学势μ增强色屏蔽、修改重夸克势与跑动耦合；β主要修正热自由能并影响等离子体熵；零温下热贡献消失，重整化自由能退化为近似库仑型介质修正静态势；有限重子密度对QQbar束缚的压制远强于动量耗散；提取了色屏蔽长度与解离尺度。

Abstract: We study heavy-quark observables including static interquark potential, thermal free energy and running coupling via a five-dimensional asymptotically AdS spacetime with translational symmetry breaking (TSB). The Einstein-Maxwell-axion geometry involves two scales: chemical potential $μ$ for finite baryon density, and TSB parameter $β$ for momentum relaxation. Numerical simulations at finite and zero temperature reveal that both $μ$ and $β$ weaken color interactions and facilitate quarkonium dissociation in strongly coupled quark-gluon plasmas through different mechanisms. The chemical potential dominates color screening and modifies the heavy-quark potential and running coupling, while $β$ mainly affects plasma entropy and corrects thermal free energy. At zero temperature, thermal contributions vanish, and the renormalized free energy becomes a medium-modified static potential with an approximate Coulombic form. Finite baryon density suppresses $Q\bar{Q}$ binding much more strongly than momentum dissipation at all temperatures. We extract the color screening length and dissociation scale, and discuss phenomenological implications for quarkonium in heavy-ion collisions. This work clarifies medium correction mechanisms for color interactions and thermodynamics, and presents a consistent picture for heavy-quark probes in dense dissipative plasmas.

Method: 基于广义仿射Springer纤维Sp_ν(\tilde{g},f)的几何结构，结合C^*不动点分解与双陪集W_ν\backslash\tilde{W}/W_f标记，建立最高权与不动点之间的映射。

Result: 每个非空C^*不动点对应一个单模，其最高权由映射\tilde w \mapsto \tilde w(kΛ_0+\tildeρ)-\tildeρ确定；不动子簇维数编码对数模等非半单结构；该框架在D_4、E_6、E_8及^3D_4、^2A_3等例子中复现了已知结果。

Conclusion: 该几何框架为非可容许W-代数的表示提供了统一理解，并揭示了其与仿射Springer几何及镜像对称的深层联系。

Abstract: Motivated by the mirror symmetry for circle compactified 4d $N=2$ theories, we propose a geometric framework for studying the representation theory of non-admissible $W$-algebras $W^{k}(\mathfrak g,f)$ at levels $k=-h^\vee+\frac{1}{n}\frac{m}{u}$, using the geometry of generalized affine Springer fibers $Sp_ν(\tilde{g},f)$ with slope $ν=u/m$. The central proposal is that each non-empty $C^*$-fixed locus, labeled by a double coset $\tilde w\in W_ν\backslash\tilde{W}/W_f$, gives rise to simple modules whose highest weight is determined by the map $\tilde w\mapsto\tilde w(kΛ_0+\tildeρ)-\tildeρ$, while the dimension of the fixed variety encodes additional non-semisimple structure (logarithmic modules). We verify this correspondence in numerous examples, including $D_4$, $E_6$, $E_8$, and twisted theories of type $^3D_4$ and $^2A_3$, where our geometric counting reproduces known results for both admissible and non-admissible $W$-algebras.

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于并行欠阻尼Langevin链的高效无权重事例生成方法，结合学习Stein差异作为收敛诊断，并用神经网络代理初始化减少精确矩阵元计算量，显著提升高重数末态事例生成效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高重数末态的精确事例生成面临矩阵元计算昂贵和拒绝采样效率低的挑战。

Method: 采用多条并行欠阻尼Langevin链，每条链仅保留一个终端状态以生成无权重事例；使用学习得到的Stein差异作为收敛判据估计弛豫时间；引入简单神经网络代理进行初始化。

Result: 在树图级 uū→Z+ng 过程中验证了方法有效性：弛豫所需精确目标Langevin步数适中，且随末态粒子数增长缓慢；神经网络代理初始化显著减少了精确矩阵元与梯度的计算次数。

Conclusion: 该方法为高精度对撞机现象学中的高效无权重事例生成提供了可行新路径，兼具计算效率与统计鲁棒性。

Abstract: Efficient event generation is a major computational challenge for precision collider phenomenology, especially for high-multiplicity final states where matrix-element evaluations are expensive and rejection-sampling efficiencies are low. We study an alternative approach based on many parallel underdamped Langevin chains, retaining one terminal state from each chain to obtain unweighted events while avoiding within-chain autocorrelation. A learned Stein discrepancy is used as a convergence diagnostic, providing a data-driven estimate of the relaxation time. We apply the method to tree-level $u\bar u\to Z+n g$ event generation and find that relaxation requires only a modest number of exact-target Langevin steps, with mild growth over the multiplicities studied. Finally, we show that simple neural-network surrogate initialization can substantially reduce the required number of exact matrix-element and gradient evaluations.

### [109] [Towards a consistent perturbation theory at finite temperature](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14863)
*Passant Ali,Peter Lowdon,Owe Philipsen*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于热粒子（thermoparticles）概念的有限温度量子场论微扰理论新框架，修正了传统Gell-Mann-Low关系在热场中的不一致推广，解决了实时间形式中病态壳层贡献和无质量理论中红外发散等问题，并通过与格点模拟对比验证了其高精度预测能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准有限温度量子场论微扰方法存在实时间形式中病态壳层贡献、无质量理论红外发散等问题，根源在于对真空Gell-Mann-Low关系的热推广不自洽——错误使用了相互作用热理论中本不存在的自由散射态。

Method: 基于非微扰谱学洞察，提出以阻尼但稳定的热激发（即热粒子）代替自由粒子构建广义Gell-Mann-Low关系；由此展开的微扰级数具有与标准方法相同拓扑结构，但传播子替换为依赖动力学的热粒子传播子。

Result: 新框架消除了标准方法中的病态壳层项和红外发散；在质量φ⁴理论中，两圈虚时间计算与格点模拟的两点关联函数高度吻合，展现出媲美真空情形的精确预测能力。

Conclusion: 热粒子微扰理论提供了自洽、无病态且高精度的有限温度量子场论微扰框架，从根本上修正了热场论基础，有望推广至更广泛理论。

Abstract: The standard approach to perturbation theory for finite-temperature quantum field theories has several issues, including the appearance of ill-defined on-shell contributions in the real-time formulation, and infrared diverges in massless theories. Earlier studies indicate that these issues all stem from the inconsistent thermal generalisation of the Gell-Mann-Low relation, which forms the foundation of perturbation theory in vacuum. This inconsistency arises from the use of free scattering states in the relation, which are known not to exist in interacting thermal theories. In this work, we propose a generalisation of the Gell-Mann-Low relation for scalar theories based on non-perturbative spectral insights, namely that finite-temperature scattering states can be described by damped but stable particle-like excitations, so-called thermoparticles. The perturbative expansion of this generalised relation gives rise to contributions with exactly the same topology as the standard finite-temperature approach, except that now the propagators appearing in this expansion are not those of a free field but of thermoparticles, which depend on the dynamics of the theory. We demonstrate that thermoparticle perturbation theory resolves the known problems of the standard approach. Furthermore, by comparing imaginary-time calculations at two-loop level with numerical lattice simulations of two-point correlation functions in massive $φ^{4}$ theory, we explicitly show that this framework gives rise to precise predictions, as in the vacuum case, in stark contrast to the standard approach.

</details>


### [110] [Why fluctuations of conserved charges in the confining regime above $T_{ch}$ behave as if the quarks were free?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15798)
*L. Ya. Glozman*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文解释了在手征交叉温度以上，守恒荷涨落表现出类似自由夸克行为的原因，而介子关联函数却显示出手征自旋和SU(4)对称性，表明传播自由度是被色电禁闭弦连接的无质量夸克。关键在于：守恒夸克数密度在时间方向不传播，但在空间方向传播，其空间传播子在T > 220 MeV时接近自由夸克环；而介子传播子则与自由夸克气体显著不同。因此，守恒荷‘看不见’禁闭，而介子关联函数能探测到禁闭。该现象类比于零温下e⁺e⁻→强子过程中的夸克-强子二象性。文章提出‘弦状流体’微观图像：即由重叠强相互作用色单态团簇组成的介质，泡利原理要求的夸克交换使夸克呈现准自由行为，反映在守恒荷涨落中。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解释为何在手征交叉温度以上，守恒荷涨落看似自由夸克行为（曾被误认为去禁闭证据），而同时介子关联函数却明确显示禁闭特征（如手征自旋和SU(4)对称性），二者表面矛盾需统一理解。

Method: 对比分析全QCD中守恒夸克数密度的空间传播子与介子传播子的行为，并与自由夸克气体（自由夸克环）模型进行定量比较；结合零温夸克-强子二象性类比，构建高温下弦状流体的微观物理图像。

Result: 发现守恒夸克数密度的空间传播子在T > 220 MeV时极接近自由夸克环，而介子传播子则与之截然不同；从而阐明守恒荷涨落不敏感于禁闭，而介子关联函数可探测禁闭；该双重行为可在‘重叠色单态团簇+夸克交换导致准自由’的弦状流体图像中得到统一描述。

Conclusion: 守恒荷涨落呈现自由夸克特征并非去禁闭的证据，而是源于其空间传播性质与禁闭机制解耦；真正的禁闭信号保留在介子关联函数中；高温强相互作用物质（T_ch < T < T_d）应理解为由强耦合色单态团簇构成的弦状流体，其中夸克因团簇间交换而呈准自由，从而协调涨落与谱函数的不同表现。

Abstract: Some cumulants of the fluctuations of conserved charges soon above the chiral crossover behave as if the quarks were free. This was taken by many as evidence of deconfinement. At the same temperatures the mesonic correlators reveal the chiral spin and SU(4) symmetries, indicating that the propagating degrees of freedom are massless quarks connected into color singlets by the chromoelectric confining string. These correlators are qualitatively different from the free quark gas. Here we clarify the reason for the difference. The conserved quark number densities do not propagate in time but do propagate in spatial directions. The mesonic propagators calculated in full QCD differ radically from the free quark loop (quark gas) above T_ch. In contrast, the quark number density spatial propagator in full QCD at T > 220 MeV is very close to the free quark loop.
  In other words, the conserved charges do not see confinement, in contrast to the mesonic correlators. This is consistent with the well understood quark-hadron duality at T=0 in e^+e^- -> hadrons, where at invariant masses above 2 GeV the cross-section in the confining regime is represented by the free quark loop plus small perturbative corrections. All these features above T_ch but below the deconfinement temperature T_d can be combined within the following microscopic picture of the stringy fluid matter. It is a medium of the overlapping strongly interacting color singlet clusters. The quark interchanges between the clusters, required by Paili principle, make the quarks quasifree, which is reflected in fluctuations of conserved charges.

### [112] [Chiral-odd structure of the $N \to Δ$ transition: tensor form factors from QCD light-cone sum rules](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.16433)
*Ulaş Özdem*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文首次使用QCD光锥求和规则直接计算了N→Δ跃迁的张量跃迁形状因子（TFFs），通过核子分布振幅和不同轻锥参数集，在1≤Q²≤10 GeV²范围内计算了四个独立TFFs，并进行了静态极限外推；发现u、d夸克对四个TFFs的贡献呈现三种不同味结构特征，为手征奇异性物理及未来横自旋相关可观测量提供模型无关输入。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 提供N→Δ跃迁中手征奇异性张量形状因子的首个直接理论计算，弥补电磁与引力跃迁之外的互补信息空白，并为横自旋相关可观测量及格点QCD验证提供基准。

Method: 采用QCD光锥求和规则，基于洛伦兹协变性、厄米性、宇称、时间反演及Rarita-Schwinger约束构建张量流矩阵元参数化形式；利用核子分布振幅（含不同扭度波函数）计算四个TFFs，并用多极拟合函数外推至静态极限；进行u/d夸克味分解分析。

Result: 在1≤Q²≤10 GeV²范围内得到四个TFFs数值结果；发现F₁、F₂以d夸克主导（|Fᵈ|≫|Fᵘ|），F₃呈近似反对称结构（Fᵘ≈−Fᵈ），F₄则u/d贡献大小相近但符号相反；揭示了与核子张量荷截然不同的夸克味行为特征。

Conclusion: 该工作为N→Δ张量跃迁提供了首个系统、模型无关的理论预言，其味结构特征具有新奇物理内涵，可作为检验格点QCD与其它唯象方法的重要基准，并支撑未来横自旋物理实验分析。

Abstract: We present the first direct calculation of the tensor transition form factors (TFFs) of the $N \to Δ$ transition using the QCD light-cone sum rules. The matrix element of the tensor current sandwiched between the nucleon and $Δ$ states is parametrized in terms of four independent form factors, derived from Lorentz covariance, Hermiticity, parity, time-reversal, and the Rarita--Schwinger constraints. The natural-parity character of the $1/2^+ \to 3/2^+$ channel combined with the spin-$1$ polarization content of the Rarita--Schwinger spinor imposes a trailing $γ_5$ in the parametrization, in analogy with the gravitational $N \to Δ$ case. Using the nucleon distribution amplitudes expanded in wavefunctions of different twists, we compute the four TFFs in the spacelike range $1 \leq Q^2 \leq 10$~GeV$^2$ for two sets of light-cone input parameters, and extrapolate to the static limit through multipole fit functions. A flavor decomposition into $u$- and $d$-quark contributions reveals three qualitatively distinct patterns among the four TFFs: $d$-quark dominance with $|F^d| \gg |F^u|$ for $F_1$ and $F_2$ -- in marked contrast to the diagonal nucleon tensor charges where the $u$-quark dominates; an antisymmetric flavor structure $F^u \approx -F^d$ for $F_3$, which naturally explains the absence of a stable isoscalar sum rule for this form factor; and comparable but opposite-sign flavor contributions to $F_4$, with a suppressed isoscalar combination. The TFFs provide chiral-odd information complementary to the electromagnetic and gravitational $N \to Δ$ transitions and offer model-independent input for future analyses of transversity-related transition observables, to be checked against lattice QCD and other phenomenological approaches.

### [113] [Pre-Training for Simulation-Based Science: A Study on Jet Foundation Model Training Objectives](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14870)
*Ibrahim Elsharkawy,Joschka Birk,Vinicius Mikuni,Wahid Bhimji,Gregor Kasieczka,Benjamin Nachman*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文系统比较了在高能物理领域中不同预训练方法（监督分类、流匹配生成、自监督掩码粒子建模）对基础模型性能的影响，发现分类预训练在标签充足时最优，而结合掩码粒子建模在低标签场景下更优；流匹配预训练仅对下游生成任务有效，且需在预训练目标中显式包含才能迁移成功。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 科学领域中高精度模拟可生成大量带标签数据，为不同于工业界自监督预训练的新范式提供了可能，亟需系统评估不同预训练目标的效果。

Method: 基于OmniLearned高能物理基础模型框架，在JetClass数据集上对比监督分类、流匹配生成和自监督掩码粒子建模（MPM）三种预训练方法，并在top jet分类和JetNet条件生成两个下游任务上进行微调评估。

Result: 1）分类预训练在标签充足时最优，MPM联合训练在低标签微调时表现最佳；2）流匹配预训练对分类任务无明显增益；3）流匹配必须作为预训练目标才能显著提升下游生成任务性能；4）分类与生成任务具有正交性，跨任务泛化需预训练目标同时涵盖二者。

Conclusion: 预训练目标需根据下游任务类型和标签可用性进行定制；在仿真驱动的科学AI中，应采用混合或任务对齐的预训练策略，并建立可控的预训练目标缩放分析范式。

Abstract: Foundation models (FMs) trained on large datasets and fine-tuned on downstream tasks have emerged as a powerful paradigm in AI for science. Industrial FMs are typically trained using self-supervision with masking due to the lack of labels. In many scientific domains, accurate simulations are plentiful and facilitate large, labeled datasets. This opens up new possibilities for pre-training. We present a systematic comparison of pre-training methods using the OmniLearned High Energy Physics FM framework. We test supervised classification, flow-matching generation, and self-supervised masked particle modeling. All models are pre-trained on the JetClass dataset and fine-tuned on two representative downstream tasks, top jet classification and JetNet conditional generation. Among other observations, for classification tasks, we find that pure classifier pre-training is optimal when downstream labels and model capacity are plentiful, but combining it with self-supervised masked particle modeling (MPM) is uniquely powerful in the low-finetuning label regime. Flow matching-based generative pre-training seems to provide little benefit for downstream classification, and interestingly, for downstream generation, we find that flow matching must be in the pre-training objective to see a significant finetuning advantage, hinting at the orthogonality of classification and generation tasks. That is, for a model to transfer to both generative and classification downstream tasks, it must be pre-trained on both. This study provides a template for controlled scaling analysis of pre-training objectives for foundation models in simulation-based sciences.

Abstract: This paper is devoted to study the spin-spinor formalism to deal with amplitudes for massive particles. For each case, we display the amplitudes using charts that represent the flow of spin/helicities from the initial to the final particles, which can be used to calculate the total squared amplitude. One can also study the symmetries of the process by comparing different branches along the charts, which are related by those symmetries. Finally, we study the massless limit of the massive theory, employing the concept of Little Group Contraction (LGC), which was used first by Inonu and Wigner to derive the algebra of the Little Group (LG) for the massless case as the limit of the massive one.

Abstract: The hadronic tensor encodes crucial information regarding the internal structure of hadrons, reflecting the non-perturbative features of quantum chromodynamics (QCD). In this work, we directly compute the hadronic tensor within (1+1)-dimensional $\rm U(1)$ and $\rm SU(2)$ gauge theories by evaluating real-time current-current correlation functions. Utilizing quantum algorithms executed on classical hardware, we demonstrate that the hadron form factors for both meson and baryon states can be reliably extracted from the hadronic tensor. With this parameter, the measured production cross sections for the $K_3^*(1780)$, $K_2(1820)$, $K_2(1770)$ and $K_4^*(2045)$ states are successfully reproduced. Employing the same framework, the production cross sections for other high-orbital kaons are predicted. The results indicate that these states possess sizable cross sections and exhibit characteristically forward-peaked angular distributions, which is a typical feature of $t$-channel exchange, highlighting their great potential for observation in future experiments.

### [126] [Parton wakes and field angular momentum in chiral QCD plasma](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15739)
*Mohammad Yousuf Jamal*

Method: 采用含贝里曲率修正的手性动力学理论，在有限μ₅、零外磁场条件下分析色场响应。

Result: 发现屏蔽部分几乎不受μ₅影响（仅通过德拜质量间接体现）；而出现线性依赖于μ₅的宇称奇横向色场结构（方位角色电场、极向色磁场、环流色电流），并由此产生一个沿部分子运动方向、奇宇称、量级为10⁻⁴–10⁻³ℏ的净场角动量。

Abstract: A fast parton moving through the quark-gluon plasma trails a wake of color fields, usually characterized through its screening cloud and the associated energy loss. Its behavior in a plasma carrying a chiral imbalance, set by a chiral chemical potential $μ_5$, remains largely unexplored, in particular whether the imbalance induces a parity-odd component in the wake. We address this within chiral kinetic theory with Berry curvature corrections, at finite $μ_5$ and zero magnetic field. The screening sector is found to be nearly insensitive to $μ_5$, which enters only through the Debye mass. The chiral imprint resides instead in a parity-odd sector, comprising an azimuthal field encircling the parton, a poloidal chromo-magnetic field, and a circulating color current. All three are linear in $μ_5$ and transverse to the velocity, and hence do no work on the parton. As the central result, these handed fields endow the wake with a net field angular momentum about the parton direction, odd in $μ_5$ and of order $10^{-4}$--$10^{-3}\,\hbar$ per parton. The chiral medium thereby opens a parity-odd channel connecting hard probes to the chiral and vortical structure of the plasma.

In this work, we formulate this transport problem with the Boltzmann equation. Its integral solution organizes successive scattering effects as a deterministic expansion in scattering orders. We find that sensitivities of $\sim 10^{-2}$--$10^{-1}$~fb are achievable for scalar masses below the $Z$ boson mass, while sensitivities of $0.1$--$1$~fb are obtained in the mass range 80--120 \GeV. Motivation: 探究双费米子产生与衰变过程中自旋密度矩阵的秩与媒介粒子自由度之间的关系，以实现对CP破坏、量子纠缠和贝尔非定域性的实验探测，并克服‘不可行定理’限制。

Method: 基于两费米子F_a F_b通过单标量或单光子交换产生与衰变的过程，分析其自旋密度矩阵ρ的秩r_ρ；结合CP对称性（守恒或破缺）推导自旋分析能力，并以η_c→ΛΛ̄（BESIII）和Higgs→ττ（LHC）、ΛΛ̄产生（BESIII）为例进行具体应用与验证。

Result: 发现单标量交换对应秩1纯态，可确定自旋分析能力并探测CP破坏；单光子交换对应秩2混合态，可完整重构自旋密度矩阵、探测纠缠与贝尔非定域性；并提出N×N自旋密度矩阵在r_ρ≤N−2时可在轻子对撞机上一般性重构的猜想。

Conclusion: 自旋密度矩阵的秩是揭示媒介粒子性质与量子关联的关键指标；该方法为高能物理中CP破坏检验、量子基础检验（如贝尔不等式）提供了新实验路径，并拓展至一般N维情形。

Abstract: Considering two-fermion $F_a F_b$ productions and decays via one scalar or photon exchange at the $e^+e^-$ collider, we show that the rank $r_ρ$ of spin density matrix $ρ$ is equal to the number of degrees of freedom of the mediator. For one generic scalar exchange, the spin density matrix is rank one for a pure state. With rank-one condition, we can determine the spin analyzing powers for $F_a$ and $F_b$ and their product if the CP symmetry is violated and conserved, respectively, and probe the CP violation. These results can be applied to the $η_c \to Λ{\bar Λ}$ at the BESIII experiment and the Higgs $\to ττ$ at the LHC. For one photon exchange, the spin density matrix is rank two for a mixed state. Considering the $Λ\bar Λ$ productions and decays at the BESIII experiment as an example, we show that the spin analyzing powers for $F_a$ and $ F_b$ can be determined by the rank-two conditions in details. Therefore, we can reconstruct the spin density matrices, probe the quantum entanglement and Bell non-locality, and evade the no-go theorem. Furthermore, we conjecture that the $N\times N$ spin density matrix with $r_ρ \le N-2 $ can be reconstructed at the lepton colliders in general.

By matching to Lattice QCD at vanishing baryon chemical potential through Lattice perturbation theory, we establish a connection between perturbative results and Lattice simulations and assess the size of higher-order corrections.   <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: π⁺π⁻不变质量谱在ρ⁰(770)以上存在多个宽且重叠的共振态，传统分波分析难以分辨，尤其在光致产生、超外围重离子碰撞和电致产生过程中；亟需新物理机制辅助分辨。

Method: 利用超外围碰撞中由量子纠缠引起的自旋干涉效应，建立角谐波Aₙ（对应cos(nΔφ)不对称性）与干涉态自旋之间的选择定则：两个自旋-1振幅干涉仅产生A₂，而自旋-1与自旋-2振幅干涉则产生A₁和A₃；结合ALICE实验在1.0–1.4 GeV/c²区间的数据进行假设检验。

Result: 两种物理图像——光核产生的自旋-1 ρ'(1450)与双光子产生的自旋-2 f₂(1270)——对不变质量谱拟合效果相当，但预测的A₁和A₃角谐波截然不同：前者A₁=A₃=0，后者呈现显著峰；该差异被ALICE数据支持，证实选择定则的有效性。

Conclusion: 该自旋干涉选择定则为超外围碰撞中的强子谱学提供了新工具，也是首次可行地分离γγ→π⁺π⁻连续过程与主导光核背景的方法，从而提供了一个干净的低能非微扰QCD探针。

Abstract: The $π^+π^-$ invariant mass spectrum above the $ρ^0(770)$ is rich with broad, overlapping resonances. Disentangling them, whether in photoproduction, ultra-peripheral heavy-ion collisions, or electroproduction, is a longstanding challenge for conventional partial-wave analysis. We show that the recently observed entanglement-enabled spin-interference effect in ultra-peripheral collisions provides a quantum-mechanical filter that resolves this ambiguity: the angular harmonics $A_n$ of the $\cos(nΔφ)$ asymmetry, which are governed by selection rules in the spin of the interfering states. Specifically, overlap between two distinct spin-1 amplitudes leads to interference that populate $A_2$ alone, while overlap of a spin-1 amplitude with a spin-2 one generates $A_1$ and $A_3$. Utilizing ALICE data in the $1.0$--$1.4\,\mathrm{GeV} \; c^{-2}$ region, we demonstrate that two physically distinct hypotheses -- an additional spin-1 $ρ'(1450)$ (produced via photonuclear interactions) versus a spin-2 (photon-photon) $f_2(1270)$ state -- fit the invariant mass spectrum equally well but predict different $A_n$: identically zero $A_1$ and $A_3$ in the spin-1 case, versus pronounced peaks in the spin-2 case. This selection rule provides a new tool for hadronic spectroscopy in ultra-peripheral collisions and the first viable route to isolating the $γγ\toπ^+π^-$ continuum from the dominant photonuclear background, revealing a clean low-energy probe of non-perturbative QCD.

</details>


### [145] [Threshold cusp effects to measure masses of radiatively decaying hadrons: The $B_{s0}^*$ mass from the $Υφ$ spectrum](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.16976)
*Hai-Long Fu,Xu Zhang,Feng-Kun Guo,Christoph Hanhart,Ulf-G. Meißner,Mao-Jun Yan*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出一种模型无关的方法，利用伴生强子与目标强子间的S波吸引相互作用，在不变质量谱中通过阈值尖峰或束缚态峰来精确测定难以探测的光子衰变强子（如Bs0*和Bs1）的质量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Bs0*和Bs1等强子主要衰变到含光子的末态，在强子对撞机上极难探测；同时它们可能具有偏离传统夸克模型的奇特性质，亟需实验确认。

Method: 基于目标强子与已知质量伴生强子之间的S波吸引相互作用，分析其末态不变质量谱在阈值处的尖峰（cusp）或略低于阈值的峰（对应束缚态），从而反推目标强子质量；以D¯DsK三体系统的一阶粒子-二聚体计算作为原理验证。

Result: 成功复现LHCb在B→KJ/ψφ中观测到的X(4274)结构，将其解释为Ds0*¯Ds阈值尖峰，得到Ds0*质量为(2322±6) MeV，与实验一致，并支持X(4274)的JPC=0−+；进一步外推至底夸克区，预言在Υφ不变质量谱中Bs0*¯Bs阈值（~11.09 GeV）附近存在类似结构。

Conclusion: 该方法为探测光子主导衰变的奇特强子（尤其是Bs0*和Bs1）提供了干净、模型无关的实验探针，有望在LHC的Υφ末态中实现Bs0*质量的精确测量。

Abstract: Hadrons that decay predominantly into final states containing photons are notoriously difficult to detect at hadron colliders. Prominent examples are the yet-unobserved $B_{s0}^*$ and $B_{s1}$, the bottom partners of the $D_{s0}^*(2317)$ and $D_{s1}(2460)$, which are expected to exhibit exotic properties deviating from the conventional quark-model predictions of $\bar b s$ mesons. We propose a general, model-independent method to overcome this problem: when the target hadron has an attractive $S$-wave interaction with a companion hadron of precisely known mass, the line shape of a suitable final state develops a cusp at the pair threshold, or a peak just below it if the attraction binds, so that subtracting the companion mass returns the target mass, up to the binding energy in the latter case. As a proof of concept, a leading-order particle-dimer calculation of the $D\bar D_s K$ three-body system reproduces the $X(4274)$ structure in the LHCb $J/ψφ$ distribution extracted from $B\to K J/ψφ$, as a $D_{s0}^*\bar D_s$ threshold cusp driven by a nearby virtual-state pole, yielding $m_{D_{s0}^*}=(2322\pm6)$ MeV in agreement with its measured value and favoring $J^{PC}=0^{-+}$ for the $X(4274)$. Transferring the elastic three-body interaction to the bottom sector, we predict an analogous structure at the $B_{s0}^*\bar B_s$ threshold near $11.09$ GeV, making the $Υφ$ invariant-mass distribution at the LHC a clean probe of the $B_{s0}^*$ mass.

</details>

Abstract: In this paper, we investigate the production of scalar singly charmed four-quark states from $B$ meson decays, employing phenomenological SU(3) flavor symmetry analysis and final-state interaction theory. Our study focuses on their production branching ratios and $CP$ violation. The results show that the branching ratios for producing either $VV$ or $PP$ molecular states from $B$ meson decays can be as large as the order of $10^{-4}$. Moreover, for processes with direct $CP$ violation, the production of $VV$ molecular states exhibits a sizable $CP$ asymmetry of order $10^{-3}$. Our findings also suggest that the recently observed $T_{\bar c\bar s 0}^*(2870)^0$ state is more consistent with the $\overline D^{*0} K^{*0}$ molecular configuration. We expect that our predictions will be validated by future experiments.

Abstract: We present a dynamical mechanism for the erasure of inflationary isocurvature perturbations of the non-compact QCD axion. The key ingredient is an early-time runaway exponential potential, which drives the axion onto the well-known scaling cosmological attractor after inflation. Once on the attractor, the axion tracks the dominant component of the Universe, radiation, and isocurvature modes are erased even if the field is effectively massless during inflation. When the QCD potential turns on, the axion carries nonzero velocity, and kinetic misalignment can become operative. The exponential potential induces residual CP violation, potentially accessible to future electric dipole moment searches. This mechanism requires that the axion be effectively non-compact over the field range relevant for its post-inflationary evolution.

Abstract: The neutrino sky below 165\,keV is yet to be explored. Here, we investigate prospects for probing this regime via neutrino capture on tritium. ### [149] [Direct High-Resolution Imaging of Earth-like Exoplanets with the Solar Gravitational Lens](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14899)
*Slava G. Turyshev*

Main category: astro-ph.IM

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种用于太阳引力透镜（SGL）高分辨率系外行星成像的标量孔径平均可观测性基准，通过建模真实地球亮度图经SGL传播、注入多种噪声与误差，并采用正则化傅里叶/维纳逆算法重建图像，评估了在特定观测条件下（如30 pc处类地行星、650 AU距离、1 m望远镜）的空间分辨能力与重建质量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为评估太阳引力透镜（SGL）在直接成像系外行星（特别是类地行星）任务中的实际成像可行性与性能极限，需建立包含真实物理效应（如光子噪声、导航误差、日冕残余等）的端到端可观测性基准。

Method: 基于真实地球亮度图，结合源-像面压缩、有限孔径SGL核、爱因斯坦环光子计数模型进行图像传播；注入多种现实干扰（光子噪声、曝光拖影、云状时变、日冕与探测器校准残差、光学算子失配、导航误差）；采用正则化傅里叶/维纳逆方法重建图像，并量化SNR、结构相似性（SSIM）、归一化RMS误差及傅里叶环相关分辨率等指标。

Result: 在基准场景下（地球半径行星、30 pc、650 AU、1 m望远镜、1800 s采样），重建图像达到SNR=6.89、SSIM=0.848、nRMSE=0.439、分辨率代理约232 km；高光子数情形下提升至SNR=10.49、SSIM=0.927、nRMSE=0.287、达199 km网格极限；证实相位对齐鲁棒叠加可克服云旋转导致的静态反演失效。

Conclusion: 该标量基准表明，在所建模条件下，SGL可恢复约200–230 km尺度的宽带空间对比度；关键需求在于时间采样、日冕与探测器校准、爱因斯坦环提取、像面计量、光学算子先验知识及动态反演能力，而非校准后的单极SGL模糊；但未验证推进、通信、日冕仪/外部遮星板传播、太阳物理多极、真实云场或完整动态反演流程。

Abstract: We present a scalar, aperture-averaged observability benchmark for resolved exoplanet imaging with the solar gravitational lens (SGL). A real Earth luminance map is propagated through a scanned SGL image plane using source-to-image-plane compression, a finite-aperture SGL kernel, and an Einstein-ring photon-count model. We inject photon noise, finite-exposure smear, cloud-like temporal variability, coronal and detector-calibration residuals, optical-operator mismatch, and navigation error, then reconstruct with a regularized Fourier/Wiener inverse. For an Earth-radius planet at 30 pc observed from 650 AU with a 1 m telescope, the projected image cylinder is 1.338 km across; a $128\times128$ raster has 10.46 m image-plane pitch, 99.55 km source pixels, and convolved-image SNR 43.16 for 1800 s per sample. With the stated ring-extraction, temporal, background, calibration, and navigation mitigations, the fiducial reconstruction reaches SNR 6.89, structural similarity 0.848, normalized RMS error 0.439, and a 232 km Fourier-ring-correlation resolution proxy. A higher-count case reaches SNR 10.49, structural similarity 0.927, normalized RMS error 0.287, and the 199 km two-pixel grid floor. Controlled cloud tests show that a static inverse fails for rotating cloudy data, whereas phase-registered robust coadds recover persistent surface-proxy structure in the scalar model. The dominant requirements are temporal sampling, coronal and detector calibration, ring extraction, image-plane metrology, optical-operator knowledge, and dynamic inversion, not calibrated monopole SGL blur. The benchmark demonstrates recoverable 200-230 km-class broadband spatial contrast in the stated scalar model, but does not validate propulsion, communications, coronagraphic or external-occulter propagation, physical solar multipoles, physical cloud fields, or a full dynamic retrieval pipeline.

We find that generally GridFire performs similarly to and requires significantly less user input and setup than these current generation nuclear network codes. Further, GridFire has been developed with a flexible "view" based physics engine that allowing researchers to implement domain specific physics without modifying the underlying source code. GridFire has been released under an open-source license, GPL v3.0, and will eventually be incorporated into the forthcoming 4D-STAR stellar structure evolution code.

### [151] [Spiking Neural Dedispersion: A Neuromorphic Fast Radio Burst Detection Pipeline](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15361)
*Alessio Magro*

Main category: astro-ph.IM

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于脉冲神经网络的实时快速射电暴（FRB）检测新方法——Spiking Neural Dedispersion（SND），在功耗、资源占用和检测性能间实现良好权衡，相比GPU方案功耗降低10–40倍。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 下一代射电望远镜的实时FRB探测受限于传统实时消色散后端高昂的成本与硬件开销，亟需低功耗、高效率的替代方案。

Method: 提出SND算法：一种基于脉冲编码滤波器组数据的分层延迟-相加树结构，支持任意试算DM网格和可配置分支因子；设计三种运行模式（二值、分级、浮点32位）以平衡资源与灵敏度；在SpiNNaker2芯片上实现完整检测流水线。

Result: 在合成Northern Cross数据上验证：浮点模式检测完整性达99.3%（功耗244 mW/波束），分级模式89.3%（61 mW），二值模式整体59.4%但对亮窄事件保持91%灵敏度（仅1.75 mW）；单芯片即可部署全流水线，48芯片系统总功耗约100–112 W，支持每板48波束。

Conclusion: SND为实时FRB探测提供了一种高度能效比的神经形态解决方案，显著降低功耗与硬件 footprint，具备在大型射电阵列中规模化部署的潜力。

Abstract: Real-time FRB detection at next-generation radio telescopes is increasingly dominated in cost and footprint by the real-time dedispersion backend. We present a complete neuromorphic FRB detection pipeline built on the Spiking Neural Dedispersion (SND) algorithm, a hierarchical delay-and-add tree that performs incoherent dedispersion on spike-encoded filterbank data, supporting arbitrary trial-DM grids and configurable branching factors. Three operating modes are evaluated, spanning a resource-sensitivity trade-off from binary thresholded accumulation to full float32 precision. Validated against Heimdall on synthetic Northern Cross filterbanks, float SND matches Heimdall at 99.3% detection completeness (244 mW per beam), graded mode achieves 89.3% at 61 mW, and binary mode reaches 59.4% overall (1.75 mW), retaining 91% sensitivity for bright, narrow events. The full pipeline fits on a single SpiNNaker 2 chip across all three modes; binary mode fits entirely within on-chip SRAM, while graded and float require external DRAM for the history buffer. On a deployed 48-chip system, total power projects to approximately 100-112 W, a reduction of order 10-40x over an equivalent GPU deployment, with 48 simultaneous beams per board.

### [152] [Transfer learning for transient search with small-field optical survey telescopes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15705)
*Kumar Pranshu,Kuntal Misra,Rithesh A,Jean Surdej,Sarvesh Kumar Yadav*

Main category: astro-ph.IM

TL;DR: 本文探讨了在光学巡天中利用迁移学习（TL）提升小望远镜瞬变源识别性能的方法，将ZTF的大规模数据上预训练的CNN模型迁移到ILMT的小样本数据上，实现了高准确率的real/bogus及多类瞬变分类。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 新或小视场巡天望远镜缺乏充足标注数据来训练监督机器学习模型，需借助迁移学习缓解数据稀缺问题。

Method: 采用迁移学习技术，将在Zwicky瞬变设施（ZTF）大数据集上预训练的卷积神经网络（CNN）模型，迁移到国际液态镜望远镜（ILMT）的小型标注数据集上，构建real/bogus分类器及3类、4类瞬变类型分类器，并通过独立t检验验证TL效果。

Result: real/bogus分类器测试准确率达97.3%，3类和4类瞬变分类器分别达92.9%和85.6%；t检验证实TL模型显著优于无TL基线模型。

Conclusion: 迁移学习可有效提升小样本天文瞬变识别任务的模型性能，为资源受限的巡天项目提供了可行的自动化解决方案。

Abstract: The advent of optical sky surveys has enabled several automated programs for searching transients. Many of these programs extensively use supervised machine learning (ML) algorithms to automate these searches. Effective implementation of such a strategy has an advantage over non-automated methods of transient search in terms of reduced manual labour and reporting latency. Training the relevant ML algorithms often requires extensive labelled training datasets that might not be readily available for new or small field-of-view survey telescopes. Transfer Learning (TL) is an ML technique that is often employed to address this issue by transferring knowledge from a pre-trained model, trained on an extensive dataset for a related task, to enhance performance on a new task with a limited dataset available. This paper demonstrates TL for a Convolutional Neural Network (CNN)-based real/bogus classifier model for transient detection between extensive publicly available image data from the Zwicky Transient Facility (ZTF) and a small and labelled dataset from the 4-m International Liquid Mirror Telescope (ILMT). The same technique was employed to train two different types of transient alert classifiers to characterise the detected candidates based on detection image stamps into 3 and 4 classes, respectively. The resulting model for the real/bogus classifier achieved an accuracy of 97.3% on the test dataset. Additionally, an accuracy of 92.9% was achieved for the 3-class classifier and 85.6% for the 4-class classifier. Furthermore, the statistical significance of the effectiveness of this technique was established with an unpaired t-test between TL models and baseline models trained without TL.

</details>


### [153] [Shigatse Astronomical Site Testing. I. Cloud-cover Climatology and Selected Local Meteorological Conditions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15839)
*Baiyu Zhang,Hejun Yang,Xiaojun Dong,Lingling Wang,Juean Luobu,Minfeng Gu,Xiyan Peng,Hao Luo,Yindun Mao,ZhaoXiang Qi,Basangzeren,Qihang He,Guojie Feng,Chunhai Bai,Ali Esamdin,Wenbo Gu,Siqi Wang,Zihuang Cao*

Main category: astro-ph.IM

TL;DR: 本文通过多源数据评估了青藏高原南部日喀则40米天文观测站的云量及气象条件，确认其为我国台址勘选网络中低纬度云量参考站，并明确了10月至5月为最佳观测期。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为在中国天文台址勘选网络中确立青藏高原南部日喀则站点的云量基准地位，开展多源云量与气象条件综合评估。

Method: 融合CALIPSO-GOCCP主动激光雷达气候数据、ISCCP被动卫星云图、日喀则气象站常规云量观测及现场气象站实测数据，进行长期（1988–2013与2024–2025）云量与气象特征分析。

Result: 日喀则年均云量为42.1%（GOCCP），10月至5月低云季平均云量26.3%，6–9月雨季达73.7%；气象站数据显示10–5月总云量≤40%的时段占比80.7%，夜间有效观测样本率达92.6%；确认日喀则为低纬度云量参考站，并识别出日喀则–阿里低云走廊。

Conclusion: 日喀则40米 site 是青藏高原南部具有明确低云观测窗口（10–5月）的优质天文候选台址，可作为中国台址网络中的低纬度云量基准，并支撑区域台址协同勘选。

Abstract: As the first paper in a Shigatse astronomical site-testing series, we present a multi-source assessment of cloud cover and selected local meteorological conditions at the Shigatse 40 m site on the southern Tibetan Plateau. The study combines CALIPSO-GOCCP active-lidar climatology, ISCCP HXG passive-satellite cloud fields, conventional total-cloud-amount observations from the Shigatse Meteorological Station, and on-site Weather Station measurements. Together, these records characterize Shigatse as a southern-plateau monsoon-transition cloud regime: the active-lidar climatology gives a moderate-to-low annual cloud fraction, and the cloudier months are concentrated in the June--September monsoon interval. In GOCCP, the annual mean cloud fraction is 42.1%, while the October--May low-cloud season has a mean cloud fraction of 26.3%, compared with 73.7% during the June--September monsoon interval. ISCCP gives higher absolute cloud fractions but supports the same seasonal phase and local spatial placement. The aligned 1988--2013 meteorological-station record gives a total-cloud-amount <=40% fraction of 80.7% during October--May, rising to 90.7% in the November--January core, and decreasing to 39.9% during June--September. The 2024--2025 Weather Station archive further shows high fractions of valid samples satisfying the adopted meteorological criteria during the low-cloud months: 92.6% for the October--May night-time proxy and 94.6% for the corresponding 24 h samples. These results identify Shigatse as a measured lower-latitude southern-plateau cloud-cover reference within China's site-testing network, with a well-defined October--May low-cloud observing period and a Shigatse--Ali low-cloud corridor for subsequent regional site testing.

</details>


### [154] [Scalable Bayesian data curation for next-generation radio experiments](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.16525)
*S. A. K. Leeney,E. de Lera Acedo,W. J. Handley,H. T. J. Bevins,G. Allen,D. Anstey,K. Artuc,G. Bernardi,M. Bucher,S. Carey,J. Cavillot,R. Chiello,A. S. Chu,W. Croukamp,J. Cumner,S. Dasgupta,A. K. Dash,D. I. L. de Villiers,J. Dhandha,A. Dragovic,J. A. Ely,A. Fialkov,T. Gessey-Jones,C. Kirkham,G. Kulkarni,A. Magro,P. D. Meerburg,S. Mittal,D. Molnar,R. S. Patel,J. H. N. Pattison,S. Pegwal,C. M. Pieterse,J. R. Pritchard,G. M. Z. Rajpoot,N. Razavi-Ghods,D. Robins,I. L. V. Roque,A. Saxena,K. H. Scheutwinkel,E. Shen,P. H. Sims,M. Spinelli,J. L. Tutt,J. Zhu*

Main category: astro-ph.IM

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种用于射电天文数据的全自动贝叶斯异常检测方法，将数据筛选直接嵌入推断过程，无需人工干预、阈值设定或主观判断，并在REACH项目一年的数据上验证了其有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 下一代射电望远镜产生海量数据，人工质量评估已不可行，但数据筛选对科学分析仍至关重要。

Method: 提出一种通用的、完全自动化的贝叶斯异常检测方法，将潜在异常指示变量在似然函数中边缘化，而非作为外部预标记；使用JAX实现GPU加速推断。

Result: 在REACH项目4655次观测（一年数据）上成功应用，能自动给出时频域的概率性数据质量评分，同时识别天气相关系统误差、仪器漂移和窄带射频干扰，并揭示数据质量与环境/仪器状态间的复杂依赖关系。

Conclusion: 该方法将数据筛选从外部人工瓶颈转变为自主的、推理层面的基础设施，为平方公里阵列（SKA）时代提供可扩展解决方案。

Abstract: Next-generation radio telescopes produce data volumes that preclude manual quality assessment, yet data curation remains essential for science. We present a general, fully automatic Bayesian anomaly-detection method for radio science experiments in which data curation is performed inside the inference: a latent anomaly indicator is marginalised in the likelihood rather than converted into an external pre-flag. Implemented in JAX with GPU-accelerated inference, the pipeline assigns probabilistic data-curation scores without prior knowledge and requires no thresholds, manual inspection, or subjective decisions. We demonstrate the method on the Radio Experiment for the Analysis of Cosmic Hydrogen (REACH), applying it to 4655 observations (one year of REACH data). The pipeline assigns scores across time and frequency, enabling identification of the optimal observations to carry forward into scientific inference while reducing the risk that contaminated data bias the result. In doing so, it simultaneously recovers weather-driven systematics, instrument-component drifts, and narrow-band radio-frequency interference, while revealing complex dependencies between data quality and environmental or instrumental state that would be difficult to uncover by manual curation alone. This turns data curation from an external manual bottleneck into autonomous, inference-level infrastructure for the Square Kilometre Array era.

</details>


### [155] [Graph Neural Networks Trained on Null Signal for Angle Reconstruction in X-ray Polarimetry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.16922)
*Vittorio Latorre,Victor Rodriguez-Fernandez,Alessandro Di Marco,Fabio La Monaca,Fabio Muleri,Paolo Soffitta*

Main category: astro-ph.IM

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于图神经网络（GNN）的方法，直接在气体像素探测器的稀疏六边形拓扑上重建光电子发射角，无需极化数据训练，但能恢复极化信号结构；虽局部角度重建误差优于传统矩方法（MoM）和CNN，但在全局偏振测量性能上表现更差，揭示了学习方法中局部精度与全局物理保真度间的权衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统CNN在非欧几里得、稀疏不规则探测器数据上引入几何偏差，会以百分比量级伪造成X射线偏振信号，严重损害测量保真度。

Method: 采用图神经网络（GNN）直接建模气体像素探测器的原生稀疏六边形拓扑；仅用非极化模拟数据训练，结合旋转数据增强、集成平均和调制感知模型选择以抑制虚假角调制。

Result: GNN在单轨迹角度重建误差上优于传统矩方法（MoM）和CNN，但在偏振测量任务中性能反而更差；在更具挑战性的幂律能谱分布下，仍对非极化和极化重建均保持与CNN相当的性能。

Conclusion: 该GNN框架作为诊断工具，凸显了基于学习的X射线偏振信号重建中局部重建精度与全局物理可解释性/偏振保真度之间的根本性权衡与局限。

Abstract: Scientific real detectors often produce sparse, irregular data defined on non-Euclidean domains, where conventional convolutional neural networks (CNNs) impose geometric biases that distort physical observables. In X-ray polarimetry, such distortions can mimic polarization signals at the percent level, critically limiting measurement fidelity. We consider a framework based on Graph Neural Networks (GNNs) for reconstructing photoelectron emission angles from Gas Pixel Detectors, operating directly on their native sparse hexagonal topology. The network is trained solely on unpolarized simulated data and integrates rotational data augmentation, ensemble averaging, and modulation-aware model selection to reduce spurious angular modulation. Despite never encountering polarized examples, the model is able to recover the overall structure of polarized signals. Compared with the classical Method of Moments (MoM), an analytical approach to track angle reconstruction, the proposed GNN achieves lower per-track error but yields worse performance for polarimetry, revealing a mismatch between local reconstruction accuracy and global polarimetric performance. Compared to CNN-based approaches, the framework shows competitive performance on both unpolarized and polarized reconstructions, despite being trained in a more challenging power-law energy distribution. These results position the method as a diagnostic tool to highlight the limitations and trade-offs of learning-based approaches for X-ray-polarimetry signal reconstruction.

</details>
